hugel.gat,51,61,0	script	#race_timer1-1	139,{

OnInit:
	hideoffnpc "#race_timer1-1";
	set $051219_mon_time_1_1,2;
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnCommandon:
	hideoffnpc "#race_timer1-1";
	set $051219_mon_time_1_1,2;
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnCommandoff:
	hideonnpc "#race_timer1-1";
	stopnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer10000:
	mapannounce "hugel.gat","The Individual Monster Race will be opened soon. We hope that everyone will join this event.",8,0x87ceeb;
	end;

OnTimer30000:
	mapannounce "hugel.gat","Individual Monster Race Arena has been opened. We hope that everyone will join this event.",8,0x87ceeb;
	set $051219_mon_time_1_1,1;
	donpcevent "Race Progress Timer::OnCommandon";
	end;

OnTimer90000:
	mapannounce "hugel.gat","The arena for Individual Monster Race has been opened. Players who want to join the race, please enter the Arena.",8,0x87ceeb;
	end;

OnTimer210000:
	mapannounce "hugel.gat","The registration period for Individual Monster Race is about to end. Please enter the arena as fast as possible.",8,0x87ceeb;
	end;

OnTimer270000:
	mapannounce "hugel.gat","The registration period for Individual Monster Race is about to end.",8,0x87ceeb;
	end;

OnTimer272000:
	mapannounce "hugel.gat","Players who wish to join the competition, please enter the arena as soon as possible.",8,0x87ceeb;
	end;

OnTimer330000:
	mapannounce "hugel.gat","The race is going to begin soon. For those who fail to join the race in time, please take part in the event next time.",8,0x87ceeb;
	set $051219_mon_time_1_1,0;
	donpcevent "#race_timer1-1::OnCommandoff";
	end;
}

// Custom name, original: Ticket Giving Service Staff <- Aegis one is too long [Tsuyuki]
p_track01.gat,73,22,1	script	Ticket Staff#single	899,{

OnInit:
	hideonnpc "Ticket Staff#single";
	end;

OnCommandon:
	hideoffnpc "Ticket Staff#single";
	end;

OnCommandoff:
	hideonnpc "Ticket Staff#single";
	end;

OnClick:
	set '@max_max_c,checkweight(1201,1);
	set '@now_weight,MaxWeight - Weight;
	if (('@now_weight < 2000) || ('@max_max_c == 0)) {
		mes "[Ticket Staff]";
		mes "Hello there!";
		mes "If you wish to join the 'Individual' Monster Race, ";
		mes "please choose one monster from ";
		mes "Monster No.1 to Monster No. 6 ~";
		next;
		mes "[Ticket Staff]";
		mes "However..";
		mes "It seems that you don't have enough space ";
		mes "to receive the monster ticket.";
		close;
	}
	set '@Luk_1,$051219_mr_1_luk1;
	set '@Tire_1,$051219_mr_1_tire1;
	set '@Luk_2,$051219_mr_1_luk2;
	set '@Tire_2,$051219_mr_1_tire2;
	set '@Luk_3,$051219_mr_1_luk3;
	set '@Tire_3,$051219_mr_1_tire3;
	set '@Luk_4,$051219_mr_1_luk4;
	set '@Tire_4,$051219_mr_1_tire4;
	set '@Luk_5,$051219_mr_1_luk5;
	set '@Tire_5,$051219_mr_1_tire5;
	set '@Luk_6,$051219_mr_1_luk6;
	set '@Tire_6,$051219_mr_1_tire6;
	set '@select,monster_race_1;
	mes "[Ticket Staff]";
	mes "Hello there!";
	mes "If you wish to join the 'Individual' Monster race,";
	mes "please choose a monster from the ";
	mes "monster no.1 to no.6 that participate in the race~";
	next;
	switch(select("View Monster Status","Monster No. 1","Monster No. 2","Monster No. 3","Monster No. 4","Monster No. 5","Monster No. 6")) {
	case 1:
		mes "Monster No. 1 [^CC6600LUK^000000 : " + '@Luk_1 + "] [^EE0000VIT^000000 : " + '@Tire_1 + "]";
		mes "Monster No. 2 [^CC6600LUK^000000 : " + '@Luk_2 + "] [^EE0000VIT^000000 : " + '@Tire_2 + "]";
		mes "Monster No. 3 [^CC6600LUK^000000 : " + '@Luk_3 + "] [^EE0000VIT^000000 : " + '@Tire_3 + "]";
		mes "Monster No. 4 [^CC6600LUK^000000 : " + '@Luk_4 + "] [^EE0000VIT^000000 : " + '@Tire_4 + "]";
		mes "Monster No. 5 [^CC6600LUK^000000 : " + '@Luk_5 + "] [^EE0000VIT^000000 : " + '@Tire_5 + "]";
		mes "Monster No. 6 [^CC6600LUK^000000 : " + '@Luk_6 + "] [^EE0000VIT^000000 : " + '@Tire_6 + "]";
		close;
	case 2:
		set '@sin_ticket,$051219_mon_time_1_1;
		if ('@sin_ticket == 1) {
			if (monster_race_1 > 0) {
				mes "[Ticket Staff]";
				mes "Hello there~";
				mes "You have chosen Monster No. ^FF0000" + '@select + "^000000.";
				mes "You will be informed through annoucement when the race begins.";
				mes "Thank you for";
				mes "your patience.";
				close;
			} else {
				mes "[Ticket Staff]";
				mes "Yes!! You have chosen Monster No. 1";
				mes "Please accept this ticket";
				mes "and wait for the race to begin.";
				mes "You will be informed through announcement";
				mes "when the race begins.";
				getitem 7514,1;
				set monster_race_1,1;
				close;
			}
		} else {
			mes "[Ticket Staff]";
			mes "I'm sorry, but a Monster";
			mes "Race is now in progress.";
			mes "If you'd like to participate, then please wait for the next race.";
			close;
		}
	case 3:

p_track01.gat,30,38,0	script	Runner No. 1 for Individual Race 	139,1,0,{

OnInit:
	hideonnpc "Runner No. 1 for Individual Race ";
	end;

OnCommandon:
	emotion ET_SURPRISE,"Runner No. 1 for Individual Race ";
	hideoffnpc "Runner No. 1 for Individual Race ";
	monster "p_track01.gat",58,38,"The 1st Racer",1725,1,"Runner No. 1 for Individual Race ::OnMyMobDead";
	end;

OnCommandoff:
	hideonnpc "Runner No. 1 for Individual Race ";
	killmonster "this",strnpcinfo(0)+"::OnMyMobDead";
	end;

OnTouchNPC:
	initnpctimer;
	set $051004_monster_race_,1;
	donpcevent "Runner No. 2 for Individual Race ::OnCommandoff";
	donpcevent "Runner No. 3 for Individual Race ::OnCommandoff";
	donpcevent "Runner No. 4 for Individual Race ::OnCommandoff";
	donpcevent "Runner No. 5 for Individual Race ::OnCommandoff";
	donpcevent "Runner No. 6 for Individual Race ::OnCommandoff";
	end;

OnTimer1000:
	mapannounce "p_track01.gat","End~ The Race has ended!!!",8,0x33FF66;
	end;

OnTimer2000:
	mapannounce "p_track01.gat","And the winner is~ Monster No. 1~!!",8,0x33FF66;
	end;

OnTimer6000:
	mapannounce "p_track01.gat","The participants who make the correct guess, please proceed to the Redemption Service Staff..",8,0x33FF66;
	end;

OnTimer8000:
	mapannounce "p_track01.gat","Prize giving to the winner will only last for 5 minutes!",8,0x33FF66;
	end;

OnTimer9000:
	donpcevent "Medal Distributor#single::OnCommandon";
	hideonnpc;
	killmonster "this",strnpcinfo(0)+"::OnMyMobDead";
	end;
}

p_track01.gat,67,45,5	script	Medal Distributor#single	845,{

	set '@max_max_c,checkweight(1201,1);
	set '@now_weight,MaxWeight - Weight;
	if (('@now_weight < 2000) || ('@max_max_c == 0)) {
		mes "[Medal Distributor]";
		mes "Before exchanging";
		mes "please take off some of the things that you're carrying.";
		close;
	}
	if (countitem(7514) > 0) {
		mes "[Medal Distributor]";
		mes "I am the Redemption Service Staff";
		mes "who will give the winner medals and ticket";
		mes "to the participants who";
		mes "make the correct guess";
		mes "for the Monster Race.";
		next;
		mes "[Medal Distributor]";
		mes "The redemption of the winner ticket of every round";
		mes "can only be made at ^0000FFthe particular round^000000.";
		mes "Please remember that.";
		mes "You can take the medal and";
		mes "find Wayne in Hugel to retrieve your prizes.";
		next;
		mes "[Medal Distributor]";
		mes "Do you want to show me your ticket?";
		next;
		set '@M_Racing1,$051004_monster_race_;
		if ('@M_Racing1 == 1) {
			if (monster_race_1 == 1) {
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";
				mes "Congratulations! You have won!";
				mes "Although the winning rate for individual is higher than the doubles,";
				mes "it's not easy to get a correct guess too..";
				mes "You're really amazing";
				next;
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";
				mes "Anyway...";
				mes "Do you want to change";
				mes "the 'ticket' into 'medal' right now?";
				next;
				switch(select("Yes","Maybe later")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[Medal Distributor]";
					mes "I will confirm your ticket now.";
					mes "Hmm, the winning monster for this round...";
					mes "Yup! That's right!";
					mes "Congratulations again!";
					next;
					mes "[Medal Distributor]";
					mes "I will give you the medal as";
					mes "the proof of the winner for the individual race.";
					mes "As for the medal, bring it to Hugel ";
					mes "and look for Wayne";
					mes "to change it into prizes.";
					mes "Please use it wisely.";
					delitem 7514,1;
					set monster_race_1,0;
					getitem 7515,4;
					close;
				case 2:
					mes "[Medal Distributor]";
					mes "The redemption of the winner ticket of every round";
					mes "can only be made at ^0000FFthe particular round^000000.";
					mes "Please remember that.";
					close;
				}
			} else {
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";
				mes "Ah, what a pity.";
				mes "I hope that you will win it next time.";
				close;
			}
		} else if ('@M_Racing1 == 2) {
			if (monster_race_1 == 2) {
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";

				mes "You're really amazing";
				next;

				mes "Anyway...";
				mes "Do you want to change";
				mes "the 'ticket' into 'medal' right now?";
				next;
				switch(select("Yes","Maybe later")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[Medal Distributor]";
					mes "I will confirm your ticket now.";
					mes "Hmm, the winning monster for this round...";
					mes "Yup! That's right!";
					mes "Congratulations again!";
					next;
					mes "[Medal Distributor]";
					mes "I will give you the medal as";
					mes "the proof of the winner for the individual race.";
					mes "As for the medal, bring it to Hugel ";

					mes "The redemption of the winner ticket of every round";
					mes "can only be made at ^0000FFthe particular round^000000.";
					mes "Please remember that.";
					close;
				}
			} else {
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";
				mes "Ah, what a pity.";
				mes "I hope that you will win it next time.";
				close;
			}
		} else if ('@M_Racing1 == 6) {
			if (monster_race_1 == 6) {
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";
				mes "Congratulations! You have won!";
				mes "Although the winning rate for individual is higher than the doubles,";
				mes "it's not easy to get a correct guess too..";
				mes "You're really amazing";
				next;
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";
				mes "Anyway...";
				mes "Do you want to change";
				mes "the 'ticket' into 'medal' right now?";
				next;
				switch(select("Yes","Maybe later")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[Medal Distributor]";
					mes "I will confirm your ticket now.";
					mes "Hmm, the winning monster for this round...";
					mes "Yup! That's right!";
					mes "Congratulations again!";
					next;
					mes "[Medal Distributor]";
					mes "I will give you the medal as";
					mes "the proof of the winner for the individual race.";
					mes "As for the medal, bring it to Hugel ";
					mes "and look for Wayne";
					mes "to change it into prizes.";
					mes "Please use it wisely.";
					delitem 7514,1;
					set monster_race_1,0;
					getitem 7515,4;
					close;
				case 2:
					mes "[Medal Distributor]";
					mes "The redemption of the winner ticket of every round";
					mes "can only be made at ^0000FFthe particular round^000000.";
					mes "Please remember that.";
					close;
				}
			} else {
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";
				mes "Ah, what a pity.";
				mes "I hope that you will win it next time.";
				close;
			}
		} else {
			mes "[Medal Distributor]";
			mes "I am the Redemption Service Staff";
			mes "who will give the winner medals and ticket";
			mes "to the participants who";
			mes "make the correct guess";
			mes "for the Monster Race.";
			next;
			mes "[Medal Distributor]";
			mes "The redemption of the winner ticket of every round";
			mes "can only be made at ^0000FFthe particular round^000000.";
			mes "Please remember that.";
			mes "You can take the medal and";
			mes "find Wayne in Hugel to retrieve your prizes.";
			close;
		}
	} else {
		mes "[Medal Distributor]";
		mes "I am the Redemption Service Staff";
		mes "who will give the winner medals and ticket";
		mes "to the participants who";
		mes "make the correct guess";
		mes "for the Monster Race.";
		next;

			delitem 7514,1;

			end;
		}
	case 2:
		mes "[Exit Guide]";

		mes "the next Monster Race.";
		close;
	}

			mes "[Eckar Ellebird]";
			mes "Ah, are you trying to get in there";

	mes "[Game Guide]";

	mes "How can I help you?";
	next;
	switch(select("What's Monster Race?","I wanna join","I want to redeem ticket")) {
	case 1:
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "Monster Race is a famous event in Hugel.";
		mes "It's a type of game where";
		mes "the kids play to relieve their boredom.";
		mes "The will use their pet";
		mes "to compete in a race";
		next;
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "As time goes bye, it became a grand event of the city.";
		mes "Finally, they build this";
		mes "Race Arena.";
		next;
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "There are Individual and Double categories";
		mes "in the monster race.";
		mes "^0000FFIndividual race refers to making the right guess for the monster that becomes the winner in the race";
		mes "^000000, Double race refers to making the right guess";
		mes "for the monster that becomes the champion and first runner up in the race";
		mes "regardless of the positioning.";
		next;
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "Initially, this is just a game and";
		mes "no items or zeny are involved in the event.";
		mes "After the arena was built,";
		mes "a small amount of entrance fee is needed";
		mes "to support the operation and pet management process.";
		next;
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "As a rebate for the entrance fee,";
		mes "participant who make the right guess for winner in individual race";
		mes "and the winner as well as first runner up in the Double Race";
		mes "will be given a small reward.";
		mes "Since making the correct guess ";
		mes "for individual race is easier compared to the Double race,";
		mes "the reward for double race is much better.";
		next;
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "As for the reward,";
		mes "^0000FFThe ticket that becomes the winning ticket in the race^000000";
		mes "must be given to the Redemption Service Staff for exchange.";
		mes " ^0000FFPlease remember that";
		mes "the ticket can only be used";
		mes "at the time after the race takes place.^000000";
		next;
		break;
	case 2:
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "You need to get a ticket";
		mes "to join the race.";
		mes "The rules of the race is to choose";
		mes "the first and second monsters that will reach the finishing point";
		mes "regardless of their position.";
		next;
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "The ticket does not require additional payment.";
		mes "It is given by the ";
		mes "Ticket Staff";
		mes "You can found it from the mini map.";
		viewpoint 1,73,22,1,0xFF3355;
		next;
		break;
	case 3:
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "When the ticket wins the race,";
		mes "you can exchange it at the redemption counter.";
		mes "^0000FFPlease take note that";
		mes "ticket redemption can only be done";

		mes "Only winning ticket can be used to redeem item.^000000";
		next;
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "In order to prepare for the next race,";
		mes "you cannot stay in the arena before the next race begins";
		mes "and you have to leave the arena after the 5 minutes redemption session.";

		mes "you will be automatically";
		mes "moved out of the arena.^000000";
		next;
		mes "[Game Guide]";
		mes "Please remember what I have said";
		mes "as you will receive certain punishment";

		next;

	mes "in the Monster Race.";
	close;
}

p_track02.gat,67,45,5	script	Medal Distributor#medal	845,{

	set '@max_max_c,checkweight(1201,1);
	set '@now_weight,MaxWeight - Weight;
	if (('@now_weight < 2000) || ('@max_max_c == 0)) {
		mes "[Medal Distributor]";
		mes "Before exchanging";
		mes "please take off some of the things that you're carrying.";
		close;
	}
	if (countitem(7514) > 0) {
		mes "[Medal Distributor]";
		mes "I am the Redemption Service Staff";
		mes "who will give the winner medals and ticket";
		mes "to the participants who";
		mes "make the correct guess";
		mes "for the Monster Race.";

		mes "find Wayne in Hugel to retrieve your prizes.";

		mes "[Medal Distributor]";
		mes "Do you want to show me your ticket?";
		next;
		set '@race_2_1,$051101_mon_race_2_1;
		set '@race_2_2,$051101_mon_race_2_2;
		if (('@race_2_1 == 1) && ('@race_2_2 == 2)) || (('@race_2_1 == 2) && ('@race_2_2 == 1)) {
			if ((monster_race_2_1 == 1) && (monster_race_2_2 == 2)) || ((monster_race_2_1 == 2) && (monster_race_2_2 == 1)) {
				mes "[Medal Distributor]";
				mes "Congratulations! You have won!";

	case 1:
		if (countitem(7514) == 0) {

			mes "Good bye.";

			end;

			mes "Monster Race Arena.";
			mes "Good bye.";
			delitem 7514,1;
			set monster_race_2_1,0;
			set monster_race_2_2,0;
			close2;
			warp "hugel.gat",63,73;
			end;
		}
	case 2:
		mes "[Exit Guide]";
		mes "I hope you will enjoy";
		mes "the next Monster Race.";
		close;
	}

	} else if ('@start > 80) && ('@start < 91) {

	}
	end;

		case 1:
			mes "[Ei felle]";

			mes "I won't have so many useless iron";

			next;
			mes "[Ei felle]";
			mes "I have sent a lot of people to ask about that special ore";
			mes "but the result is nothing...How disappointing...";
			next;
			break;
		}
		if (countitem(7515) > 0) {
			mes "["+ strcharinfo(0) +"]";
			mes "Excuse me, is this the medal that you mentioned just now...";
			next;

			case 1:
				mes "[Ei felle]";

				mes "and it can be made use to ";
				mes "produce good product.";
				next;
				mes "[Ei felle]";

				mes "What should I give you...";
				next;
				switch(select("Please provide aid in future experience","Help me with the job NPC","Work harder in your research","Ask about progress of research")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[Ei felle]";
					mes "Hmmm...This is nothing important.";
					mes "Anyway, let me pray for your safety";
					mes "and hopefully it will be helpful";
					mes "for your future adventure!";
					next;
					mes "[Ei felle]";
					mes "Hmmmm.....Hahaha!!!";
					gmcommand "@emotion ET_HUK";
					emotion ET_HUK,"Ei felle#repay01";
					next;
					mes "[Ei felle]";
					mes "Phew, that's it.";
					mes "I pray that your future will be blessed";
					mes "with safety and happiness.";
					delitem 7515,1;
					if (BaseLevel < 21) {
						set BaseExp,BaseExp + 150;
					} else if ((BaseLevel > 20) && (BaseLevel < 31)) {
